-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `patient_master`
--

CREATE TABLE `patient_master` (
  `id` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `patient_id` varchar(36) DEFAULT NULL,
  `person_name` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `mobile_number` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `pimage_path` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `age` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `gender` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `house_no` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `street_locality` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `place_tehsil` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `district_city` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `pin_code` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `state_ut_province` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `country` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `latitude` float NOT NULL,
  `longitude` float NOT NULL,
  `quarantined_type` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `maritial_status` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `occupation` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `aadharcardnumber` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `symptom` varchar(30) NOT NULL,
  `police_station` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `isforeignreturn_foreigner` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `dateofarrival` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `datetillquarantined` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `port_of_originofjourney` varchar(60) DEFAULT NULL,
  `port_of_finaldestination` varchar(60) DEFAULT NULL,
  `finaldistrict_city` varchar(60) DEFAULT NULL,
  `country_of_originofjourney` varchar(60) DEFAULT NULL,
  `country_of_finaldestination` varchar(60) DEFAULT NULL,
  `last_latitude` float DEFAULT NULL,
  `last_longitude` float DEFAULT NULL,
  `reasonforquarantine` varchar(60) DEFAULT NULL,
  `incontactsuspecttype` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `status` varchar(30) DEFAULT NULL,
  `category` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `parentid` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `imei` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `device_id` varchar(30) DEFAULT NULL,
  `userid` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `createddate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `appregdate` datetime DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `primary_secondary_contacts`
--

CREATE TABLE `primary_secondary_contacts` (
  `id` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `contact_mobile_number` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `contact_name` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `contact_address` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `type_of_contact` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `contact_description` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `mobile_number` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `userid` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `createddate` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `zone` varchar(60) DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `quarantine_history`
--

CREATE TABLE `quarantine_history` (
  `id` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `mobile_number` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `qtimestamp` datetime NOT NULL,
  `latitude` float NOT NULL,
  `longitude` float NOT NULL,
  `image_path` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `userid` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `createddate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `zone` varchar(60) DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;
